                     <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="2094">
                      THE BEAUTIFUL, UPDATED Garden Suite is a perfect retreat for travelers, visiting parents or executives. It is private, secure and well managed so that you won't have to worry about food in the frig or clothes in the closets. Nestled in a 1912 Arts and Crafts-style home, this apartment has an open and spacious design, artful touches and comfy, elegant furnishings. We love to travel ourselves, so we try to think of everything our guests will need. Just bring a suitcase!
                     </div>
                     <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="2095">
                      This is a completely private mother-in-law unit in a 1912 home. Although it is spacious with 2 bedrooms and a large bath, full kitchen, eating area and living room, we prefer to rent to only 1-2 people to keep the property tranquil for everyone. We do accept 3 guests max for an additional $30/nt charge. For comfort and ambiance during cold winter evenings, we have a gas heating stove in the living room that has the warmth of a hearth. In the summer, the apartment stays relatively cool so that a/c is really not necessary. Please note that although the unit does connect to our upstairs space with a staircase, we keep doors locked when we host guests so that the space and both entries are entirely private. The entry from the street is well-lit at night and has it's own outdoor seating area. The apartment has another private entry/exit to the backyard, where in the summer you might enjoy a game of bocce or sit for spell in our large backyard. All in all, you will love this cozy and beautiful space that is much more personal and intimate than a commercial hotel.
                     </div>
                     <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="2096">
                      We are 10 minutes due east of downtown traveling by car on 17th Street. Directly to the west is the lovely Johnson and Wales campus just two blocks away, and Park Hill, one of Denver's oldest and most elegant neighborhoods is also to the west. Park Hill features some lovely parkways, including 17th Street, Montview Boulevard, 23rd Street and Monaco Boulevard; it is a nice place to walk. (And if you're really motivated, the Zoo, City Park and Museum of Nature and Science are about 2.5 miles west.) To the north and south are the relatively newer neighborhoods of Stapleton and Lowry, with town centers, restaurants and cafes. Going to the east, the neighborhoods are more transitional, but changing fast as they are now anchored by the newer and huge Anshutz Medical Campus. Not to be missed is the spanking new Stanley Marketplace, housed in a former airplane factory, with brewpubs and some of the most innovative new restaurants in Denver. I-70, the main route to the mountains, is also nearby, approximately a 2 mile drive to the north.
